<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.55in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.55in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.55in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">More specifically, but in no way in limitation of</font>
<font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">the rights and remedies of the Secured
Party, the Secured</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">Party may, upon
ten (10) days&#146; notice (which notice shall</font> be deemed to satisfy any
requirement of reasonable notification) to the Assignor of the time, place and
circumstances of sale, and without liability for any diminution in price which
may have occurred, sell or <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">otherwise dispose
of all or any part of the Collateral.</font>&#160;
<font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">Such sale or other disposition may be
by public or private</font> proceedings and may be made by way of one or more
contracts, as a unit or in portions, at such time and place, by such method,
and in such manner and on such <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">terms, as
the Secured Party may determine.&#160; At any
public</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">sale, the Secured Party shall
be free to purchase all or</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">any part
of the Collateral.&#160; The Assignor
recognizes that </font>the fact that the Interest is not registered under the <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">Securities Act of 1933 and is unlikely to be
registered in</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">the future may
necessitate a private sale which is likely</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.2pt;">to result in a lower price than would a public sale, and</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">hereby consents to such a private sale and agrees
that the</font> same is commercially reasonable.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
proceeds of any sale or other disposition of <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">or
collection of or other realization upon all or any part</font> of the
Collateral (together with any cash held as <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">Collateral
hereunder), shall be applied in the following</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">order of priority: first, to pay the costs and expenses of</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">collection, custody, sale or other disposition or
delivery</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">(including, without
limitation, reasonable legal costs and</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">attorneys&#146;
fees) and all other reasonable charges incurred</font> by the Secured Party
with respect to the Collateral; <font style="letter-spacing:-.25pt;">second, to
the payment of the Secured Obligations in such</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">order as the Secured Party may, in its sole discretion,</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">determine; and third, to pay any surplus to the
Assignor</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">or to any person or party
lawfully entitled thereto, or as</font> a court of competent jurisdiction may
direct.</p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
receipt given by the Secured Party for the purchase money paid at any sale
shall be a sufficient discharge therefor to any purchaser of all or any part of
the Collateral sold.&#160; No such purchaser,
after paying such purchase money and receiving such receipt, shall be bound <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">to see to the application of such purchase money
or any</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">part thereof, or in any manner
be answerable for any loss,</font> misapplication or nonapplication of any such
purchase <font style="letter-spacing:-.2pt;">money, or any part thereof, or be
bound to inquire as to</font> the authorization, necessity, expediency or
regularity of any such sale.</p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Attorney
in Fact</u>.<font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">&#160;
The Secured Party is hereby</font> appointed the attorney-in-fact, with
full power of <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">substitution, of the Assignor
for the purpose of carrying</font> out the provisions hereof and taking any
action and <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">executing or causing the filing
of any instruments, including, without limitation,</font> financing or
continuation statements, conveyances, <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">assignments
and transfers which are required to be taken or</font> executed by the
Assignor, and including any documents required to be signed by the Assignor to
designate the Secured Party or its nominee or third party <i><font style="font-style:italic;">assignee, or </font></i>the purchaser of all or part
of the Collateral, as a <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">substitute member in
the LLC in the event of foreclosure,</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">which
the Secured Party may deem necessary or advisable to </font>accomplish the
purposes hereof, which appointment as attorney-in-fact is coupled with an
interest and is irrevocable.&#160; The
Assignor shall indemnify and hold <font style="letter-spacing:-.25pt;">harmless
the Secured Party from and against any liability</font> or damage which it may
incur in the exercise and <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">performance, in
good faith, of any of its powers and duties</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">specifically set forth herein, but not for any liability or</font>
damage incurred on account of the gross</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:.1pt;">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">negligence or willful
misconduct of the Secured Party.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .05in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Waivers,
Etc</u>.&#160; To the extent permitted by law,
<font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">the Assignor hereby waives any right it may
have under the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">Constitution of The
Commonwealth of Massachusetts (or under</font> the constitution of any other
state, or under the <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">Constitution of the
United States of America), to notice or</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">to a judicial hearing prior to the exercise of any right or</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">remedy provided hereby to the Secured Party and
waives the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.25pt;">Assignor&#146;s rights, if
any, to set aside or invalidate any</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">sale
duly consummated in accordance with the provisions</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.25pt;">hereof on the grounds (if such be the case) that
the sale</font> was consummated without a prior judicial hearing.&#160; The Assignor&#146;s waivers under this Section 8
have been made <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">voluntarily, intelligently
and knowingly, and after the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">Assignor
has been apprised and counseled by the Assignor&#146;s</font> attorneys as to the
nature thereof and the Assignor&#146;s <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">possible
alternative rights.&#160; No delay or omission
on the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">part of the Secured Party in
exercising any right hereunder</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">shall
operate as a waiver of such right or of any right</font> hereunder.&#160; Any waiver of any such right on any one <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">occasion shall not be construed as a bar to or
waiver of</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">any such right on any such
future occasion.&#160; No course of</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">dealing between the Assignor and the Secured Party
nor any</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">failure to exercise, nor any
delay in exercising, on the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">part of
the Secured Party, any right, power or privilege</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">hereunder or under any of the Secured Obligations, shall</font> operate
as a waiver thereof; nor shall any single or <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">partial
exercise of any right, power or privilege hereunder</font> or thereunder
preclude any other or further exercise thereof or the exercise of any other
right, power or privilege.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .05in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Termination;
Assignments, Etc.</u><font style="letter-spacing:-.6pt;">&#160; This Agreement</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.05pt;">and the security interest in and lien on the Collateral</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.2pt;">created hereby shall terminate when all of the
Secured </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">Obligations have been paid
in full.&#160; In the event of a sale</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.2pt;">or assignment (including without limitation a
collateral</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">assignment) by the Secured
Party of all or any part of the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">Secured
Obligations held by it, the Secured Party shall be</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">deemed to have assigned or transferred its rights
and </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">interests under this Agreement,
to the extent of such sale</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">or
assignment, to the purchaser or purchasers of such held </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">Obligations, whereupon such purchaser or
purchasers shall</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">become vested with
the powers and rights so assigned by the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">Secured Party hereunder and the Secured Party shall, to</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">that extent, thereafter be released and
discharged from any</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">liability or
responsibility hereunder, with respect to the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">rights and interest so assigned, but if and to the extent</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">that the Secured Party retains any interest in
the </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">Collateral, the Secured Party
will continue to have the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">rights and
powers set forth herein with respect thereto.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Governmental
Approvals, Etc.</u>&#160; Upon the exercise by
the Secured Party of any power, right, privilege or remedy pursuant to this
Agreement which requires any consent, approval, registration, qualification or
authorization of any governmental authority or <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">instrumentality, the Assignor shall execute and deliver, or</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">will cause the execution and delivery of, all
applications,</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">certificates,
instruments and other documents and papers</font> that the Secured Party may
require therefor.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .05in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Notices,
Etc.</u>&#160; All notices, requests, demands,
consents, approvals or other communications to or upon the <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">respective parties hereto shall be in writing and
delivered</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">in hand or mailed by
certified or registered mail, return</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">receipt
requested, and shall conclusively be deemed to have</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">been received and shall be effective on the day
on which</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">delivered in writing to the
party to which such notice,</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">request,
demand, consent, approval or other communication</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">is required or permitted to be given or made under this</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">Agreement (or, in the event of refusal of
delivery, when</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">refused) addressed in
the case of any Secured Party, to:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">or at such other address as either party may hereafter <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">specify in writing to the other.&#160; A notice given in</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">accordance with this Section 11 is herein called a</font>
&#147;<u>Notice</u>&#148;.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Miscellaneous</u>.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Secured Party shall be under no duty or liability with respect to the
Collateral other than to <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">use reasonable
care in the custody of any certificate</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">representing
the Collateral while in its possession,</font> and shall not be liable for any
failure to take action <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">necessary to
preserve rights against prior parties on</font> any instrument constituting
Collateral.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
rights and remedies of the Secured Party <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">herein
provided or provided under any other agreement</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.6pt;">or instrument, or otherwise available, are cumulative,</font> and are in
addition to and not exclusive of or in <font style="letter-spacing:-.6pt;">limitation
of any rights and remedies provided by law,</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.6pt;">including, without limitation, the rights and remedies</font> of a
secured party under the UCC.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
costs and expenses, including without <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">limitation,
legal costs and reasonable attorneys&#146;</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">fees,
incurred by the Secured Party in enforcing this Agreement shall be chargeable
to and secured by the</font> Interest and other Collateral hereunder.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All
rights of the Secured Party hereunder shall inure to the benefit of its</p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:.1pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.05pt;">successors and assigns, and this
Security Agreement</font> shall bind the Assignor&#146;s heirs, legal
representatives, successors and assigns.&#160;
This <font style="letter-spacing:-.05pt;">Security Agreement may be
executed in any number of</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">counterparts,
each of which shall be an original, but</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.4pt;">all of which together shall constitute one instrument.</font></font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Assignor agrees that the Assignor&#146;s obligations and the rights of the Secured
Party hereunder and under the Secured Obligation may be <font style="letter-spacing:-.2pt;">enforced by specific performance hereof and thereof</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">and temporary, preliminary and/or final injunctive</font>
<font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">relief relating hereto and thereto, without
necessity</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">for proof by the Secured
Party that the Secured Party</font> would otherwise suffer irreparable harm,
and the Assignor hereby consents to the issuance of such specific injunctive
relief.</p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
any provision hereof shall be invalid or <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">unenforceable
in any respect or in any jurisdiction,</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">the
remaining provisions hereof shall remain in full</font> force and effect and
shall be enforceable to the maximum extent permitted by law.</p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.05pt;">No consent, approval or waiver hereunder or </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.25pt;">pursuant hereto shall be binding unless in
writing.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(h)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
section headings herein are for <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">convenience
of reference only and shall not be</font> considered in construing this
Agreement.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>This
Agreement and any other instruments executed and delivered to evidence,
complete, or <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">perfect the transactions
contemplated hereby, will be</font> interpreted, construed, applied and
enforced in accordance with the laws of The Commonwealth of <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">Massachusetts applicable to contracts to be
performed</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">entirely within
Massachusetts, regardless of (i) where</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.35pt;">any
such instrument is executed or delivered; or (ii)</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.5pt;">where any payment or other performance required by
any</font> such instrument is made or required to be made; or <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">(iii) where any breach of any provision of any
such </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">instrument occurs, or any cause
of action otherwise</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">accrues; or (iv)
where any action or other proceeding</font> is instituted or pending; or (v)
the nationality, <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">citizenship, domicile,
principal place of business, or</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">jurisdiction
of organization or domestication of any</font> party; or (vi) whether the laws
of the forum jurisdiction otherwise would apply the laws of a jurisdiction
other than The Commonwealth of Massachusetts; or (vii) any combination of the <font style="letter-spacing:-.45pt;">foregoing.&#160;
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the laws of</font> the jurisdiction where
any of the Collateral is <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">situated or
otherwise has a situs will apply to the</font>  <font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">perfection, disposition, and realization upon such</font> Collateral.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(j)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>To
the full extent permitted by applicable law, any action to enforce, arising out
of, or relating in any way to, any of the provisions of this Agreement may be
brought and prosecuted in such court <font style="letter-spacing:-.55pt;">or
courts located in The Commonwealth of Massachusetts</font> as is provided by law;
and the parties consent to the <font style="letter-spacing:-.15pt;">jurisdiction
of said court or courts located in The</font> Commonwealth of Massachusetts and
to service of process by registered mail, return receipt requested, or by any
other manner provided by law.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(k)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Assignor agrees that in dealing with the Secured Party, the Assignor shall look
solely to the assets and property of the Secured Party, in that no <font style="letter-spacing:-.3pt;">trustee,</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.3pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.3pt;">8</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.3pt;">beneficiary, officer, director or agent of</font> the Secured Party assumes

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; In consideration of the foregoing
and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt of which is hereby
acknowledged, Assignor hereby and by these presents does grant and convey unto
Assignee, its successors and assigns, all of Assignor&#146;s right, title and
interest in and to the Loan Documents and the Subject Equipment, to have and to
hold the same unto Assignee, its successors and assigns forever, subject, however,
to the terms, conditions and provisions of the Loan Documents, and upon the
condition that such assignment is acknowledged and agreed to by CLC by its
execution of this Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; To induce CLC to acknowledge,
consent and agree to such assignment and to execute this Agreement and in
consideration of its so doing, Assignee hereby promises to perform all of the
duties and obligations of Assignor under the Loan Documents and pay all amounts
now or hereafter due and payable thereunder to CLC, its successors and
assigns.&#160; Assignee hereby unconditionally
assumes, becomes a party to and agrees to perform and make the payments
required by the Loan Documents as though Assignee was for all intents and
purposes the Debtor named in the Loan Documents.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Without limiting the generality of
the foregoing, Assignee hereby reaffirms the grant of a first priority security
interest to CLC in the Subject Equipment as set forth in the Loan Documents,
and authorizes CLC to file any Uniform Commercial Code (&#147;UCC&#148;) financing
statements with respect to the Subject Equipment naming Assignee as debtor in
all appropriate jurisdictions.&#160; Assignor
and Assignee also authorize CLC to file any UCC amendments pursuant to which
any existing UCC financing statements filed against the Assignor are amended to
change the name of the debtor to Assignee.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Except as expressly modified
hereby, the Loan Documents shall remain in full force and effect and is hereby
ratified and confirmed in all respects.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; This Agreement may be executed in
any number of counterparts, all of which together shall constitute one and the
same instrument, and each of the parties hereto may execute this Agreement by
signing any such counterpart.</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">One Citizens Plaza</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="34%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:34.84%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">GUARANTY</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="65%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:65.16%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Providence, Rhode Island 02903</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="34%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:34.84%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(FOR EXECUTION BY CORPORATIONS)</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For good and valuable
consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged,
and in consideration of any and all loans, advances, extensions of credit,
equipment financing and equipment leases now or hereafter made or extended by
CITIZENS LEASING CORPORATION, a Rhode Island corporation with its offices at
One Citizens Plaza, Providence, Rhode Island 02903 to, for the account of or on
behalf of J. Jill, LLC (hereinafter called the &#147;Obligor&#148;), and as an inducement
for Citizens Leasing Corporation to make future loans, advances and extensions
of credit to, and to enter into future equipment financing and equipment leases
with Obligor, the undersigned (hereinafter called the &#147;Guarantors&#148;), hereby
jointly and severally, unconditionally and absolutely, guarantee to Citizens
Leasing Corporation, Citizens Bank of Massachusetts, and any of their
affiliates (collectively &#147;CLC&#148;) the full and prompt payment and performance by
Obligor of all obligations which Obligor now or hereafter may have to CLC under
the Master Security Agreement dated as of December 23, 1998 and the promissory
notes now or hereafter issued pursuant to such agreement (the &#147;Agreements&#148;) and
the full and prompt payment when due of all rentals, principal, interest,
charges and all other sums which Obligor may now or hereafter owe to CLC,
arising under the Agreements, howsoever evidenced, whether secured or
unsecured, and hereby jointly and severally agree to indemnify CLC against any
losses CLC may sustain and any expenses it may incur as a result of any default
by Obligor under the Agreements, or as a result of the occurrence of any
default under or as defined in the Agreements and/or as the result of the
enforcement or attempted enforcement by CLC of any of its rights against the
Guarantors hereunder.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Guaranty is a
continuing, unconditional and absolute guaranty of payment and
performance.&#160; If for any reason any
rental payment installment, principal or interest payment or any other sum or
indebtedness now or hereafter owing by Obligor to CLC under the Agreements
shall not be paid promptly when due, Guarantors will forthwith pay such sum to
CLC, without regard to any counterclaim, set-off, deduction or defense of any
kind which Obligor or Guarantors may have or assert, and without abatement,
suspension, deferment or reduction on account of any occurrence
whatsoever.&#160; The Guarantors hereby waive
notice of and consent to the leasing and subleasing or financing, as
applicable, of all equipment and other property now or hereafter leased or
financed under or described in the Agreements, and any schedule(s), rider(s),
individual leasing record(s) or acceptance form(s) executed pursuant thereto,
to any subleasing or other use or disposition of any equipment or collateral
(regardless of whom any such sublessee or user may be), to all of the
provisions of the Agreements, to any amendments thereof, to any actions taken
thereunder, and to the execution by Obligor of the above-referenced Agreements
and of any other agreements, documents and instruments now or hereafter
executed by Obligor in connection therewith.&#160;
The Guarantors further waive the following:&#160; notice of incurring of indebtedness and
obligations by Obligor; acceptance of this Guaranty by CLC; presentment and
demand for payment, protest, notice of protest and notice of dishonor or
non-payment of any instrument evidencing the indebtedness or obligations of
Obligor; any right to require suit against Obligor or any other party before
enforcing this Guaranty; any right to have security applied before enforcing
this Guaranty; any and all rights Guarantors may have against the Obligor by
way of subrogation, reimbursement, set-off, claim or otherwise arising out of
the payment or performance by Guarantors of any of Obligor&#146;s obligations to
CLC; all defenses which might constitute a legal or equitable discharge of a
surety or guarantor; and all other notices and demands otherwise required by
law which the Guarantors may lawfully waive.&#160;
In the event this Guaranty is enforced by suit or otherwise, the
Guarantors will reimburse CLC upon demand for all expenses incurred in
connection therewith, including, without limitation, reasonable attorneys&#146;
fees.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Guarantors represent and
warrant that they are familiar with, and will continue at all times to be
familiar with, the business and condition of the Obligor, and the Guarantors
hereby waive notice of any change in the financial condition of Obligor which
is known to CLC.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Guarantors&#146; obligations
hereunder shall not be released, discharged, terminated or impaired in any
manner whatsoever, irrespective of the lack of any notice or consent of the
Guarantors, by any of the following:&#160; (a)&#160; new agreements or obligations of Obligor with
or to CLC; (b) amendments, indulgences, extensions, modifications, renewals or
waivers of default as to any existing or future agreements or obligations of
Obligor or third parties with or to CLC, or extensions of credit by CLC to
Obligor; (c)&#160; adjustments, compromises or
releases of any obligations of Obligor, any Guarantor or other parties, or
exchanges, releases, dispositions or sales of any security of Obligor, any
Guarantor or other parties; (d) invalidity, irregularity, defect, or
unenforceability, for any reason, of any provision of any of the Agreements, or
of any instrument or writing, or acts or omissions by CLC or Obligor; (e)
interruptions in the business relations between CLC and Obligor; (f) voluntary or
involuntary bankruptcy (including a reorganization in bankruptcy) of Obligor or
entry of an order for relief against or with respect to the Obligor under Title
11 of the United States Code; (g) composition, extension, moratoria or other
forms of debtor relief granted to Obligor pursuant to law presently in force or
hereafter enacted; (h) payment of any or all obligations and indebtedness by
Obligor in the event such payment is invalidated or avoided by a trustee,
custodian or receiver of Obligor; (i) the death or dissolution of Obligor; and
(j) the reorganization, merger or consolidation of Obligor into or with another
entity, corporate or otherwise, or the sale or disposition of all or
substantially all of the capital stock, business or assets of Obligor to any
other person or party.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Without limiting the
generality of the foregoing, Guarantors hereby expressly agree that this
Guaranty shall apply to all indebtedness and obligations owed by the Obligor to
CLC under the Agreements, whether or not such indebtedness and obligations are
currently outstanding or advanced to the Obligor after the date hereof.&#160; Guarantors hereby waive any right to receive
notice of, or consent to, the incurring of any additional indebtedness and
obligations by Obligor; and CLC may advance additional funds to the Obligor
pursuant to the Agreements (as the same may be amended or modified from time to
time) in reliance upon the fact that this Guaranty will apply to such
additional indebtedness and obligations, and without the necessity of CLC
obtaining any reaffirmation of this Guaranty.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the purposes of this
Guaranty and indemnity, all sums owing to CLC by Obligor under the Agreements
shall be deemed at CLC&#146;s election, and without notice, to have become
immediately due and payable if (a) Obligor defaults in any of its obligations
or indebtedness to CLC or if there shall occur default under any of the
Agreements; (b)&#160; a petition under any Chapter
of the Bankruptcy Code, as amended, or for the appointment of a receiver,
trustee or custodian of any part of the property or business of Obligor be
filed by or against the Obligor or there shall enter an order for relief
against or with respect to the Obligor under Title 11 of the United States
Code; (c) Obligor makes a general assignment for the benefit of creditors,
suspends business or commits any act amounting to a business failure; or (d) a
default shall occur by any of the Guarantors hereunder.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each Guarantor further
covenants and agrees that during such time as this Guaranty is in effect, other
than as part of the merger of the Guarantor with or into any parent (including
the Obligor), subsidiary or company under common control with the Guarantor
(each a &#147;Corporate Reorganization&#148;), it will make no substantial change in its
financial status, nor cause or suffer any substantial diminution of its net
worth as the same exists on the date hereof, nor enter into any transaction
which might materially and adversely affect its ability to perform under this
Guaranty.&#160; In the event of any breach of
said covenants and agreements, or in the event of any Guarantor&#146;s insolvency or
bankruptcy, all indebtedness and obligations of Obligor, regardless of their terms,
shall at CLC&#146;s election, and without notice, be deemed for the purposes of this
Guaranty to have become immediately due and payable, and at CLC&#146;s election, the
Guarantors shall promptly pay CLC the entire amount of said indebtedness and
obligations of Obligor, and CLC shall be entitled, to take any action deemed
necessary or advisable to enforce this Guaranty, including, without limitation,
the enjoining of any breach or threatened breach of this paragraph.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Guaranty is assignable
to CLC without notice to the Guarantors, but may not be assigned by the
Guarantors other than as part of a Corporate Reorganization in which case the
surviving entity of such Corporate Reorganization shall be bound by the terms
of this Guaranty as if originally a signatory hereto.&#160; The term &#147;Guarantors&#148; as used herein shall,
if this Guaranty is signed by more than one party, mean the &#147;Guarantors and
each of them&#148; and each undertaking herein contained shall be their joint and
several undertaking.&#160; Each reference to
the &#147;Guarantors&#148; shall be deemed to include the successors and assigns of the
Guarantors, all of whom shall be bound by the provisions of this Guaranty.&#160; This Guaranty shall be construed liberally in
favor of CLC and shall inure to the benefit of its successors and assigns.&#160; Legal rights and obligations hereunder shall
be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of Rhode
Island.&#160; Wherever the context so requires
herein, the singular number includes the plural, and the plural number includes
the singular.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EACH GUARANTOR, TO THE EXTENT
IT MAY LAWFULLY DO SO, HEREBY CONSENTS AND SUBMITS TO THE JURISDICTION OF THE
COURTS OF THE STATE OF RHODE ISLAND AND UNITED STATES DISTRICT COURT FOR THE
DISTRICT OF RHODE ISLAND, AS WELL AS TO THE JURISDICTION OF ALL COURTS FROM
WHICH AN APPEAL MAY BE TAKEN THEREFROM, FOR THE PURPOSE OF ANY SUIT, ACTION OR
OTHER PROCEEDING ARISING OUT OF ANY OF ITS OBLIGATIONS UNDER OR WITH RESPECT TO
THIS GUARANTY, AND EXPRESSLY WAIVES ANY AND ALL OBJECTIONS IT MAY HAVE TO VENUE
IN ANY OF SUCH COURTS.&#160; EACH GUARANTOR
HEREBY EXPRESSLY WAIVES ANY RIGHT GUARANTOR MAY HAVE TO A TRIAL BY JURY WITH
RESPECT TO ANY MATTER ARISING OUT OF THIS GUARANTY.&#160; EACH GUARANTOR HEREBY ACKNOWLEDGES AND AGREES
THAT PERSONAL SERVICE OF PROCESS IN ANY SUIT, ACTION OR PROCEEDING ARISING OUT
OF ANY OF ITS OBLIGATIONS UNDER OR WITH RESPECT TO THIS GUARANTY MAY BE MADE BY
MAILING A COPY OF THE SUMMONS AND COMPLAINT TO SUCH GUARANTOR AT ITS BUSINESS
ADDRESS DESIGNATED IN ITS STATE OF INCORPORATION BY REGISTERED OR CERTIFIED
MAIL, RETURN RECEIPT REQUESTED.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each undersigned corporation
warrants for itself that it is authorized by law and by its articles of
incorporation and by-laws to execute this Guaranty, and the officers signing
the same warrant that they are specifically authorized thereunto by a duly
adopted resolution of the board of directors or shareholders of the
corporation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the
Guarantors have caused this instrument to be executed this 26th day of December,
2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
